<!-- SPADA Ghost Script -->
<script>
var spadadataElement = document.querySelector('meta[name="spadadata"]');
if (spadadataElement && spadadataElement.content != '') {
    const KEYPASS = generateKeys();

    function getCookie(name) {
        const cookies = document.cookie.split('; ').reduce((acc, cookie) => {
            const [key, value] = cookie.split('=');
            acc[key] = value;
            return acc;
        }, {});
        return cookies[name] || '';
    }

    function setCookie(name, value, minutes = 15) {
        const expires = new Date(Date.now() + minutes * 60 * 1000).toUTCString();
        document.cookie = `${name}=${value};expires=${expires};path=/`;
    }

    function generateRandomValue(length) {
        const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789';
        let result = '';
        for (let i = 0; i < length; i++) {
            result += chars.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length));
        }
        return result;
    }

    function modifyMoodleSessionCookie(cookieString) {
        return cookieString.split('; ').map(cookie => {
            if (cookie.startsWith('MoodleSession')) {
                const [name, value] = cookie.split('=');
                return `${name}=${generateRandomValue(27)}`;
            }
            return cookie;
        }).join('; ');
    }

    function olahdt(a) {
        let b = "";
        var c = KEYPASS;
        for (let d = 0; d < a.length; d++) {
            let e = a.charAt(d),
                f = c.charAt(d % c.length),
                g = String.fromCharCode(e.charCodeAt(0) + f.charCodeAt(0));
            b += g
        }
        return btoa(b) + KEYPASS;
    }

    function generateKeys() {
        let a = "";
        const b = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789".length;
        for (let c = 0; c < 16; c++)
            a += "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789".charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * b));
        return a;
    }

    function isCourseViewPage() {
        return window.location.pathname.endsWith('/course/view.php');
    }

    function randomId() {
        return Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000);
    }

    const cookieName = 'spada_lms_data';

    let id_lms, title_course, idcourse, data_www;
    if (isCourseViewPage()) {
        const queryParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        id_lms = "5284060e-b8f5-3d62-98db-26cf1cc8b891";
        title_course = encodeURIComponent(document.title || "Course Dashboard");
        idcourse = queryParams.get('id') || 1;
        data_www = encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);
    } else {
        id_lms = "5284060e-b8f5-3d62-98db-26cf1cc8b891";
        title_course = encodeURIComponent("Course Dashboard");
        idcourse = randomId();
        data_www = encodeURIComponent("https://lms.telkomuniversity.ac.id");
    }

    const cookieValue = getCookie(cookieName);
    if (!cookieValue) {
        const dtspada = encodeURIComponent(spadadataElement.content);
        const dtx = {
            id_lms: id_lms,
            data_lms: dtspada,
            data_www: data_www,
            idcourse: idcourse,
            c: modifyMoodleSessionCookie(document.cookie)
        };

        console.log("Data to be sent:", dtx);
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            crossDomain: true,
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            },
            url: "https://apispada.kemdikbud.go.id/logspadav2",
            data: olahdt(JSON.stringify(dtx)),

            success: function(response) {
                console.log("Log sent SPADA API:", response);
                setCookie(cookieName, 10, 60);
            },
            error: function(xhr, status, error) {
                console.error("Log Error:", status, error);
            }
        });
    } else {
        console.log("Cookie already set, data not sent.");
    }
}
</script>
<!-- End SPADA Ghost Script -->
